    const paidData = {
        isLoggedIn: false,
        isPaying: false,
        terms: [],
        resources: [],
        onetPremiumExpireDate: null
    };

    function readCookie(name) {
        // 
        const cookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(function(row) {
            return row.startsWith(name + '=');
        });
        if (cookie) {
            return decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]);
        }

        return undefined;
    }

    try {
        var cookie = readCookie('user_data');
        if (cookie) {
            var userData = JSON.parse(cookie);
            if (userData) {
                paidData.isLoggedIn = true;
                paidData.isPaying = userData.isPaying;
                paidData.terms = userData.termIds;
                paidData.resources = userData.resourceIds;
                paidData.onetPremiumExpireDate = userData.onetPremiumExpireDate;
            }
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.error(e);
    }

    
    
    dlApi.keyvalues = dlApi.keyvalues || {};
    dlApi.keyvalues.isLoggedIn = paidData.isLoggedIn;
    dlApi.keyvalues.isPaying = paidData.isPaying;

    dlApi.keyvalues.resources = paidData.resources;

<script>
  function loadScript(src, callback) {
    let s,r,t;
    r = false;
    s = document.createElement('script');
    s.async = true;
    s.src = src;
    s.onload = s.onreadystatechange = () => {
      if (!r && (!this.readyState || this.readyState == 'complete')){
        r = true;
        callback();
      }
    };
    t = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
    t.parentNode.insertBefore(s, t);
  }

  function hideButtonForPremiumUser() {
    if (document.cookie.match('prm_sub=1')) {
      const buySubscription = document.querySelector('#buy-subscription');
      buySubscription.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    }
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', function() {
    loadScript('https://ocdn.eu/faktucs/loginbar/5_2_7_loginbar.js', () => {
       const domElement = document.getElementById('loginBar');
       const loginBar = new LoginBarSdk('https://businessinsider.com.pl', 'www.businessinsider.com.pl.okonto.front.onetapi.pl', false, false, false, true);
       loginBar.setConfiguration({
         initElement: 'text',
         defaultAvatarSvg: '<svg viewBox="0 0 18 20"><use xlink:href="#ico-loginbar-profile-blue"></use></svg>',
         modal: {
           links: [
             { icon: null, text: 'Twoje dane', url: 'https://konto.onet.pl/dashboard', class: 'full-width centered'},
             { icon: null, text: 'Zmień hasło', url: 'https://konto.onet.pl/change-password', class: 'full-width centered'},
             { icon: null, text: 'Twoja Subskrypcja', url: 'https://konto.onet.pl/subscriptions', class: 'full-width centered'}
           ]
         }
       });
       loginBar.setCustomModalRendering(renderModal);
       loginBar.init(domElement);
    });
    hideButtonForPremiumUser();
  });
    
  function renderModal() {
    const container = document.createElement('div');
    container.classList.add('loginbar-container');

    /* Profile info */
    const profileInfo = document.createElement('div');
    profileInfo.classList.add('loginbar-profile-info');
    const loggedAsInfo = document.createElement('div');
    loggedAsInfo.classList.add('loginbar-logged-as');
    loggedAsInfo.innerHTML = "Witaj!<br><b>"+this.user?.login+"</b>";

    if (this.user.avatar) {
      const avatarImage = document.createElement('img');
      avatarImage.src = this.user?.avatar;
      avatarImage.alt = 'profile image';
      profileInfo.appendChild(avatarImage);
    } else {
      const avatarDefault = document.createElement('div');
      avatarDefault.className = 'loginbar-modal-icon';
      avatarDefault.innerHTML = '<svg viewBox="0 0 18 20"><use xlink:href="#ico-loginbar-profile-blue"></use></svg>';
      profileInfo.appendChild(avatarDefault);
    }

    profileInfo.appendChild(loggedAsInfo);

    /* Custom links */
    const links = document.createElement('div');
    links.classList.add('loginbar-links');
    const linksList = this.configuration.modal.links || [];
    linksList.forEach(link => {
      const linkElement = document.createElement('div');
      linkElement.className = 'link ' + link.class;

      if (link.id) {
        linkElement.setAttribute('id', link.id);
      }

      if (link.icon) {
        const icon = document.createElement('span');
        icon.classList.add(link.icon);
        linkElement.appendChild(icon);
      }

      const hyperlink = document.createElement('a');
      hyperlink.href = link.url;
      hyperlink.innerText = link.text;
      linkElement.appendChild(hyperlink);

      links.appendChild(linkElement);
    });

    const logoutButton = document.createElement('div');
    logoutButton.className = 'logout-button';
    logoutButton.innerText = 'WYLOGUJ SIĘ';
    logoutButton.addEventListener('click', async (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      await this.accountLogout.call(this.accountLoginConfig);
      window.location.reload();
    });

    container.appendChild(profileInfo);
    container.appendChild(links);
    container.appendChild(logoutButton);

    
    document.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
      if(
        !container.contains(event.target)
        && !this.initialElement.contains(event.target)
        && container.classList.contains('show')
      ) {
        container.classList.toggle('show');
      }
    });
    

    this.initialElement.after(container);
    const logout = document.querySelector('#logout');

    if (logout) {
      logout.addEventListener('click', async (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        await this.accountLogout.call(this.accountLoginConfig);
        window.location.reload();
      });
    }
  }
  document.addEventListener('paywall.analytics.completed', function() {
      if(paywall.user.isPaying) {
          const buySubscription = document.querySelector('#buy-subscription');
          buySubscription.innerText = 'Premium';
          buySubscription.href = 'https://businessinsider.com.pl/premium';
      }
  });
  hideButtonForPremiumUser();
</script>

 var _SG_LOADER = {
     IMAGE: 'https://ocdn.eu/businessinsider/static/sg-loader/bi_hp_desktop.jpg',
     BACKGROUND_IMAGE: 'https://ocdn.eu/businessinsider/static/sg-loader/bar_background.png',
     BAR_IMAGE: 'https://ocdn.eu/businessinsider/static/sg-loader/bi_logo_sgLoader.png',
     URL_PARAM: '/najnowsze?fromscroll=1',
     ELEMENT_QUERY: '.footer_wrapper',
     TEXT: 'Przejdź do najnowszych artykułów...'
 };

 var footer = document.querySelector(_SG_LOADER.ELEMENT_QUERY);

 function loadSGScript() {
     var sgLoaderScript = document.createElement('script');
     sgLoaderScript.type = 'text/javascript';
     sgLoaderScript.src = 'https://ocdn.eu/businessinsider/static/sg-loader/sg-loader.min.js';
     sgLoaderScript.async = true;
     document.body.appendChild(sgLoaderScript);
 }

 var scriptObserverCallback = function(entries, observer) {
     entries.forEach(function(entry) {
         if (entry.isIntersecting) {
             loadSGScript();
             observer.disconnect();
         }
     })
 };
 if (window.IntersectionObserver) {
     var lazyScriptObserver = new IntersectionObserver(
         scriptObserverCallback,
         {
             rootMargin: '1000px',
             threshold: 0.01
         }
     );
     lazyScriptObserver.observe(footer);
 } else {
     loadSGScript();
 }
</script>
